  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer12803928128066302098">This summer, I’d planned to celebrate my eighteenth birthday in Europe with my fellow Manhattanites—Taddy Brill, Blake Morgan, and Vive Farnworth—until I caught my boyfriend screwing my mother.   <span id="freeText12803928128066302098" style="display:none">This summer, I’d planned to celebrate my eighteenth birthday in Europe with my fellow Manhattanites—Taddy Brill, Blake Morgan, and Vive Farnworth—until I caught my boyfriend screwing my mother. According to the police report, this vomit-inducing incident happened around the same time I’d supposedly blown-up my mother’s penthouse. Like I’m walking around Soho with a stick of dynamite in my Louis Vuitton purse—not! Now, my besties and I are in jail.<br /><br />Officer Ford Gotti, the Harley-wheelin’ biker cop who arrested us, keeps sticking his perfectly-sculpted nose into my case. His inked body is jacked like a superhero, and he says I can trust him. He wants me to fess up. I won’t. Not again. Why should I? My friends and I had a previous stint in juvie that nearly destroyed us. I gotta protect them and keep my mouth shut. Right? —Lex Easton, women’s studies major, motorcycle enthusiast, and virgin. <br /><br />The Undergrad Years is a New Adult contemporary miniseries about first loves, independence, and everlasting friendships. Contains mature content intended for readers 17 and up.</span>

        <a title="Amrutha Ram" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amrutha Ram" href="/user/show/19235474-amrutha-ram">Amrutha Ram</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer957080667" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11059298208901405533">I received this book for the exchange of an honest review.<br/><br/>Unfortunately, I was unable to finish this book, because it was honestly just so awful. The writing is sad, the characters drive me nuts, the plot is all over the place. In reality this should have 0 (on my blog, -7) stars, but that isn't an option here. <br/><br/>The book begins with Alexandra Easton, or Lex, who is apparently so chubby that her boyfriend tells her she needs to lose weight before he dare have sex with her. lol. what. Okay, so this</span>
  <span id="freeText11059298208901405533" style="display:none">I received this book for the exchange of an honest review.<br /><br />Unfortunately, I was unable to finish this book, because it was honestly just so awful. The writing is sad, the characters drive me nuts, the plot is all over the place. In reality this should have 0 (on my blog, -7) stars, but that isn't an option here. <br /><br />The book begins with Alexandra Easton, or Lex, who is apparently so chubby that her boyfriend tells her she needs to lose weight before he dare have sex with her. lol. what. Okay, so this girl who is apparently going to Columbia in the fall and has movie star parents has a low enough self esteem to sit there and take this kind of emotional abuse. Alright, I guess. So then, when she's finally getting close to losing the weight necessary to lose her "Lady V" (virginity), she comes home, to find what? Her mom and boyfriend going at it. I guess after this her (whatever was left of her) self respect kicked in, and she decides to dump her boyfriend.<br /><br />Now comes the real kicker. After she breaks up with her boyfriend, for no real reason, she decides to burn a dress and some pictures in the bathroom OF A NEW YORK CITY PENTHOUSE. Clearly little Miss Columbia isn't as smart as we thought. Anyway, I guess her mom had 02 tanks around her house to help with her youth and beauty or some equivalent bullshit, and boom, her house blows up, and Lex and her friends are arrested.<br /><br />While she's getting arrested, by the way, she flirts with the cop.<br /><br />Because after a few weeks of trying, I was unable to finish the book, I figured I'd skip to the last few chapters to find out if the book had a chance of getting any better. Hint: it didn't, it turned into some sick version of mommy porn that no one should ever have to be subjected to reading.<br /><br />I'll tell you right now, don't read this book if you want your eyesight to work fully afterwards. The poor writing style combined with the way too out there plot and the most annoying characters on the planet manifests itself in this book, Love, Lex. Hopefully I am able to avoid all Avery Aster books in the process.<br /><br />This book is marked DNF, for did not finish. (Note: This is the first book in over 6 years I have not finished).<br /><br />I received this book for the exchange of an honest review.<br /></span>

</a><br/><br/>Having read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17553217.Undressed__The_Manhattanites___1_' title='Undressed (The Manhattanites, #1) by Avery Aster' rel='nofollow noopener'>Undressed</a>, I was instantly ready for more Lex. Lex is ready to give her Lady V to her boyfriend, Kelle, but she discovers that this douche-nozzle is already balls deep into her mom. On the verge of eighteen, Lex is on the move. On to big and better things... but before she goes, a bonfire of a few bad memories sounds like a good idea... until it isn't and things go <b>boom!</b><br/><br/>But before Lex and the gang are thrown behind bars </span>
  <span id="freeText4874933205038455893" style="display:none"><i> ARC received from author in exchange for an honest review. </i><br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/92365175@N06/13807565293" title="Screenshot_1 by Charlie___Tango, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397342514i/9265679.jpg" width="410" height="480" alt="Screenshot_1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Having read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17553217.Undressed__The_Manhattanites___1_" title="Undressed (The Manhattanites, #1) by Avery Aster" rel="nofollow noopener">Undressed</a>, I was instantly ready for more Lex. Lex is ready to give her Lady V to her boyfriend, Kelle, but she discovers that this douche-nozzle is already balls deep into her mom. On the verge of eighteen, Lex is on the move. On to big and better things... but before she goes, a bonfire of a few bad memories sounds like a good idea... until it isn't and things go <b>boom!</b><br><br>But before Lex and the gang are thrown behind bars and forced into tacky orange jumpsuits, she meets Officer God. Ford has this girl spinning all sorts of crazed fantasies as she is threatened with charges of arson and attempted murder. But in her defense, he's fuck hot and she is desperately out of sugar...<br><br>Avery Aster can spin an erotic story into something sassy, snarky and all kinds of cray-cray hilarious. The one thing you know when you start a book from this author is that you will laugh. Stretching the canvas of Fiction taut as she writes. Lines are crossed, boundaries are pushed... her imagination should come with a flippin' warning label. <br><br>This little novella gives you pretty much a day in the life of one of the fab-gals of The Manhattanites. And as Lex is forced to face the music, before all is set right, she meets the hunky officer that has her exchanging her desire for candy for something a bit harder...and bigger. Ford was a fun character that had you thinking sweet and dirty thoughts that might just get you out of your next speeding ticket. Although I would have loved to have seen their story go a little further, my heart was lost to the Prince a long time ago.<br><br>This author is one of those that you just know is going to put a smile on your face when you pick up one of her books. Between the heavy panting and a bit of sweaty fun, this woman delivers humor in a major way.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7555265170342578966">Initial thoughts: <br/><br/> WHAT THE FUCK OF ALL FUCKS AM I READING?!?!?! <br/><br/>Seriously, it's what I would imagine it must feel like to have a bipolar, schizo with mania consume one of every drug on the planet, wash it down with a bottle of vodka, and then jump out of an airplane without a parachute. <br/><br/>It's like "Clueless" meets "Days of Our Lives" set to a biker ninja porno. I dunno?!? <br/><br/>I need a fucking translator; a mediator; a therapist; & a priest, rabbi, Swahili medicine man, bishop, and preacher. <br/><br/>I need a</span>
  <span id="freeText7555265170342578966" style="display:none">Initial thoughts: <br /><br /> WHAT THE FUCK OF ALL FUCKS AM I READING?!?!?! <br /><br />Seriously, it's what I would imagine it must feel like to have a bipolar, schizo with mania consume one of every drug on the planet, wash it down with a bottle of vodka, and then jump out of an airplane without a parachute. <br /><br />It's like "Clueless" meets "Days of Our Lives" set to a biker ninja porno. I dunno?!? <br /><br />I need a fucking translator; a mediator; a therapist; &amp; a priest, rabbi, Swahili medicine man, bishop, and preacher. <br /><br />I need a Xanax the size of New York! <br /><br />I need... Hell, I don't even know what I need my brain is so overloaded trying to keep up with this MC's spastic teen lingo thoughts. <br /><br />Despite, the absolute craziness, the quirky MC can be rather witty in her thoughts <i>at times. </i> ... <b>initially! </b> <br /><br />Some reviewers found humor here. Even in the initial chapters, I didn't find any of it funny. Instead, I found it entertaining in the way some people often find crazy bloopers with a kid wearing a banana costume cracking his ass after trying to take a leap from his roof to the pool. You don't laugh... You just watch the train wreck. <br /><br />The blurb mentions Rachel Van D. .......THIS IS NOT Rachel Van D's brand of SNL lol funny! No! Just no! <br /><br /><b>From Quirky Crazy To Fucking Absurdly Weird</b> <br /><br />The first part is crazy in a mildly entertaining way... 'Omg... 'Wtf' kinda way that's delivered with a healthy dose of snarky quirkiness. <br /><br />Then, around the time officer God makes his first appearance, this story takes a very wrong turn in an absurdly ridiculous way that makes me pity the keystrokes it took to write this mess. <br /><br />Btw how is Gotti shortened to God? Anyway...<br /><br />It quickly becomes nonsense for the sake of nonsense. <br /><br />The wet dreams that go on for pages upon pages were absurd and weird, not hot. <br /><br />The bike sex scene was absurd and weird, not hot. <br /><br />The HEA was weird and absurd, not swoony. <br /><br />The male mc was weird, not swoony. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marie  Brown (Marie&#39;s Tempting Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marie  Brown (Marie&#39;s Tempting Reads)" href="/user/show/7458345-marie-brown-marie-s-tempting-reads">Marie  Brown (Marie&#39;s Tempting Reads)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer877810114" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14570542609771888273">Marie's Tempting Reads Review:<br/><br/>Since I have read two books by Avery Aster, Undressed and Unscrupulous and enjoyed both, I knew I could NOT turn down an opportunity to read and review Love, Lex. When I first was gifted with this beautiful box set, I first had to take a few moments to admire this yummy cover before flying to Avery Aster's story, Love, Lex.<br/>I found this story to be funny with plenty of snark, and with a GORGEOUS biker cop being involved, this just made it absolutely DELIC!<br/>I can't say</span>
  <span id="freeText14570542609771888273" style="display:none">Marie's Tempting Reads Review:<br /><br />Since I have read two books by Avery Aster, Undressed and Unscrupulous and enjoyed both, I knew I could NOT turn down an opportunity to read and review Love, Lex. When I first was gifted with this beautiful box set, I first had to take a few moments to admire this yummy cover before flying to Avery Aster's story, Love, Lex.<br />I found this story to be funny with plenty of snark, and with a GORGEOUS biker cop being involved, this just made it absolutely DELIC!<br />I can't say I was fond of the whole drug use in the book, but since it contained a LOT of humor and a smokin' hot cop, I have to say it was easy to overlook the whole drug use thing..plus there wasn't an over abundance of it in the book which definitely helped.<br />I really liked Lex. She is curvy, spirited, amusing, and just has such a strong loyalty to her friends and people she cares about. Now with sexy Officer Gotti, he was just the perfect male specimen. Sexy, charming, concerned, and dominating..*sigh* like I said, PERFECT.<br />Lex and her friends reminded me of a mix between rich gang members and teenage Kardashians. They stick together and I totally dig that. I did NOT like how some of the people in the book considered Lex to be fat..WHAT?! I thought she was GORGEOUS just the way she was.<br />I give Love, Lex a FOUR AND A HALF STARS OUT OF FIVE because of its humor, sexiness, panty melting sex, and one drool worthy cop. I can sum this book up in one word...YUM! If your looking for a laugh out loud, sexy read then I suggest you pick up this incredible box set and read Love, Lex..plus with many other fantastic books and one low price, you definitely can't go wrong.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>

<span id="freeTextContainer996944357535245692">**CAUTION: SPOILERS AHEAD**<br/><br/>Hi Happy Readers- I received this book as an ARC from the author this morning. <br/><br/>I was so stoked to read it, I literally read it in a few hours. <br/><br/>Holy Fuckity Shit Fuck, Batman! *FANS SELF* That was hot as hell! Please note that blames just might randomly start in your pants by reading this book. Literally CALIENTE!<br/><br/>Before we get to the hotness- let me just comment on the Spice Girls and the Dawson's Creek omega reference that just made me swoon all over the fucking place.</span>
  <span id="freeText996944357535245692" style="display:none">**CAUTION: SPOILERS AHEAD**<br /><br />Hi Happy Readers- I received this book as an ARC from the author this morning. <br /><br />I was so stoked to read it, I literally read it in a few hours. <br /><br />Holy Fuckity Shit Fuck, Batman! *FANS SELF* That was hot as hell! Please note that blames just might randomly start in your pants by reading this book. Literally CALIENTE!<br /><br />Before we get to the hotness- let me just comment on the Spice Girls and the Dawson's Creek omega reference that just made me swoon all over the fucking place. That was amazing balls! And made my mother fucking week. Avery Aster- you just made me a life long fan yo! <br /><br />OK- Enough! Excuse me as I leash my inner 7th grader and calm her the fuck down!<br /><br />She's calmed the fuck down but unfortunately, I, Melissa Ann, 29 year old woman am not so calmed in the nether regions. This book is insanely HOT HOT HOTTTTTTT! Like hose me down in the backyard because the fire alarm just went off in my pants. <br /><br />The story is pretty uniquely fucked up. We have our lovely curny (curvy and horny) rich girl, Lex. Its been a really long time since I read a great curny girl novel! :)<br /><br />Can I just stop to state that our heroin is a curvy girl and there is a Spice Girls reference in this book AND its fucking witty. You should be sold on getting the book already. BUT if you aren't- then proceed with the review.<br /><br />She on the cusp of her 18th birthday. She's going to get ready for her date with her high school weekend heart Kelle. And then she hears her mother going at it in the house. Thinks mother of it until she hears her boy friends voice. QUE QUE WHAT? Yea man- I didn't even see that one coming. <br /><br />So homegirl Lex is not well in the head. Proceeds to stare at her bf and her mum go at it like bunnies. Tis tre fucked up. PLUS she was planning on giving her V card aka Lady V to her bf soon. Yikes! You really felt for her. I do have to say that scene with the watching her bf and mom get it on went on a little too long for me and made me feel extremely uncomfortable. I was super antsy and wished for Lex to SNAP THE FUCK OUT OF IT and walk the fuck out. Because it was super le gross. Ew!<br /><br />* sigh * One would think well the bad part of this book already happened and I can't get any worse. Oh no boo boo! It does. Turns out Lex and her GBF, VBF and BBF end up getting pulled over by Ford, the hunky cop who sets his eyes on the prize. And the prize is Lex. But before that happens the gang goes to jail. It becomes a little touch and go there. Friends reveal disloyalty. Again- you feel for this curvy girl.<br /><br />Let's go back to Ford real quick. Oh Ford! *swoons* Buh bye Lady V. Hip hip HURRAY for Ford! He rescues our curny heroine and you just can't help but love the cop. <br /><br />The ending was pretty great. Almost perfect. Loved it. It wraps up the story well, leaves you wanting more- thus Undergrad Years #2.<br /><br />You did a good job Avery Aster! All in all, Love, Lex is amazingly naughty book that makes me want to relive my undergrad years with Lex as my BF4L (best friend for life)!<br /><br />Happy Reading,<br />Mel<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12381347437074210227">3.5 stars I was a bit worried that these books would be toned down because of the New Adult Category, Thankfully I couldn't have been more WRONG! You get the same Sassy, Snarky, Hilarious HOTNESS that you have come to expect from Avery 's writing, just with younger characters involved. This book tells of the week Lex Easton turns eighteen. She comes home to find her mother having sex with her boyfriend Kelle.(Who is a Major ASS by the way, HATE him!) Little did she know that the best thing she e</span>
  <span id="freeText12381347437074210227" style="display:none">3.5 stars I was a bit worried that these books would be toned down because of the New Adult Category, Thankfully I couldn't have been more WRONG! You get the same Sassy, Snarky, Hilarious HOTNESS that you have come to expect from Avery 's writing, just with younger characters involved. This book tells of the week Lex Easton turns eighteen. She comes home to find her mother having sex with her boyfriend Kelle.(Who is a Major ASS by the way, HATE him!) Little did she know that the best thing she ever did was to move on from the guy who made her feel so HORRIBLE, and UNATTRACTIVE. (So Glad she didn't end up giving her Lady V to him.)In a fit while moving out, she unknowingly blows up her mother's penthouse. This is how she meets officer Hottie, I mean Gotti or Ford. Even though Lex is in so much trouble, that doesn't stop her from having some serious fantasies about Officer Gotti. (Can you BLAME her?) He was so SWEET!! He made her feel Beautiful and Good about herself for the first time. LOVE him!!! Every Curvy Girl needs a Ford in her life. Will Lex's fantasies about officer Gotti become a reality? How will Lex get out of this whole Arson Mess? You will just have to read LOVE Lex and find out. If you are looking for a quick, fun read that is both HOT and Hilarious, then this is the book for you. The only negative thing I have to say about this book is it left me wanting more. I wanted to know more about what happened in Lex and Ford's relationship. Although, I LOVE Prince Masi, and I am happy Lex found her happy ever after, part of me is SAD that it wasn't with Ford. Thank you Avery Aster. I was not disappointed. I look forward to not only the rest of the Undergrad Series, but also the rest of the Manhattenites as well. Ebook provided by Xpress reads in exchange for a honest review.</span>

<div id="review_909060946" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/909060946" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3341252-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451829371p2/3341252.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/909060946?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3341252-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer909060946" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13212908583415667665">(Read this review and more at <a href='http://prettybookmarks.wordpress.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pretty Bookmarks</a>)<br/><br/><b>
  <i>Disclaimer: I received a review copy c/o of the Publisher via Xpresso Book Tours.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Okay, I’ve said it before. When it comes to New Adult, I tend to tread lightly. Before I begin, I’d like to remind you again that this does contain mature content so reader discretion is advised.<br/><br/>When I first read the synopsis, that was what pulled me in. It sounded like Gossip Girl with a bit more pizzazz. Unfortunately, it didn’t live up to the expectation I was ha</span>
  <span id="freeText13212908583415667665" style="display:none">(Read this review and more at <a href="http://prettybookmarks.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Pretty Bookmarks</a>)<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Disclaimer: I received a review copy c/o of the Publisher via Xpresso Book Tours.</i>
</b><br /><br />Okay, I’ve said it before. When it comes to New Adult, I tend to tread lightly. Before I begin, I’d like to remind you again that this does contain mature content so reader discretion is advised.<br /><br />When I first read the synopsis, that was what pulled me in. It sounded like Gossip Girl with a bit more pizzazz. Unfortunately, it didn’t live up to the expectation I was having.<br /><br />Love, Lex follows the story of Lex, who is desperate to lose her virginity to her boyfriend — only to find him fooling around with her mother. Later, while attempting to burn some old memories, Lex ends up blowing her mother’s penthouse down and getting thrown into jail.<br /><br />Truthfully, I enjoyed the premise of it and I enjoyed the writing. It was witty and funny, which really added to the characterization of Lex. The concept and premise of the book was really interesting. Considering that this was a novella and only seven chapters long, it had pretty good content and was sufficient.<br /><br />What took away the enjoyment for me was sadly, the sex. Now, don’t get me wrong, I’ve read New Adult and had my two-off trial with Erotica so sex isn’t essentially the issue. But Lex reeked of desperation. She was so thirsty for sex that it became an eventual turn off. For somebody who is still a virgin, she knows a lot about sex (not that it’s a bad thing) and fantasizes a lot about it (and very quickly). The ending was alright for me, I kind of wanted more for Lex and felt that she deserved better.<br /><br />Is this a book for everyone? Maybe, maybe not. But it doesn’t hurt for you to try.</span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3873813725630995658">Are you a fan of the Manhattanites series? Then you going enjoy the Undergrad Years.<br/><br/>We know Lex Easton is a no holds bar and bull kind of gal in the big wide world of fashion, but what was she like before all the blood sweat and tears of becoming that world famous fashion designer?<br/><br/>I am guessing Lex was probably born kicking and screaming that the world was going to know who she was. Always in the shadow of her famous parents she had to make sure she stood out!<br/><br/>Coming home to a heartbreaking scena</span>
  <span id="freeText3873813725630995658" style="display:none">Are you a fan of the Manhattanites series? Then you going enjoy the Undergrad Years.<br /><br />We know Lex Easton is a no holds bar and bull kind of gal in the big wide world of fashion, but what was she like before all the blood sweat and tears of becoming that world famous fashion designer?<br /><br />I am guessing Lex was probably born kicking and screaming that the world was going to know who she was. Always in the shadow of her famous parents she had to make sure she stood out!<br /><br />Coming home to a heartbreaking scenario, Lex packs her bags, deciding that her friends Taddy, Vive and Blake are the only people she can trust.<br /><br />But her plans are swiftly halted when an almost tragic accident puts Lex's mother in the hospital and she is the prime suspect.<br /><br />Read about how friendships are strained, parental bonds are questioned and how Lex fantasises about what she'd like to do with the hot motorcycle cop who has apprehended her.<br /><br />Pure naughtiness and tongue in cheek humour, the Avery Aster story telling we have all grown to love! A great story about a sassy young woman and a hot Harley riding cop! Loved it!!</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1629218343" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1629218343" />
    <a title="Julie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3691807-julie"><img alt="Julie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1469974701p2/3691807.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1629218343?book_show_action=true">May 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julie" href="/user/show/3691807-julie">Julie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/21894625-love-lex">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3691807-julie?shelf=book-in-exchange-for-review">book-in-exchange-for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3691807-julie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3691807-julie?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3691807-julie?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3691807-julie?shelf=first-in-a-series">first-in-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3691807-julie?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1629218343" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12617447237848000096"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444234937i/16472991.jpg' width='150' height='50' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'll be honest, I only made it about halfway through this book and I just couldn't do it. I couldn't turn another page, I could read even another word. I. Was. Done. I had to put it down because I totally checked out.<br/><br/>This is my first and last book by Avery Aster. Sometimes I'll give an author another shot if I was a bit on the fence about the first novel that I read by them but I wasn't on the fence this time. I was over that fence and four states away. It did not go well. Unfortunately, this is</span>
  <span id="freeText12617447237848000096" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444234937i/16472991.jpg" width="150" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'll be honest, I only made it about halfway through this book and I just couldn't do it. I couldn't turn another page, I could read even another word. I. Was. Done. I had to put it down because I totally checked out.<br><br>This is my first and last book by Avery Aster. Sometimes I'll give an author another shot if I was a bit on the fence about the first novel that I read by them but I wasn't on the fence this time. I was over that fence and four states away. It did not go well. Unfortunately, this is not going to be one of my gushing reviews. This one is going to be rough. <br><br>The book is just all over the damn place. I couldn't keep up with what was happening ... it was like a tweaking hummingbird just flitting from one topic to the next. It caused a serious case of reading whiplash coupled with a healthy dose of disinterest. It reads almost as if it's a jumble of thoughts that weren't fully explored and with each disjointed sentence, you're just pulled further into this vortex of confusion. <br><br>It sure as hell doesn't help that this book is written using the urban dictionary for every other word. Everything is in such heavy slang that was uper-cray (did I use that correctly?) and nothing was jelly (again, I don't know if this is the right context, I had to Google this shit to see what it meant), forreals (this has to be another language altogether). I just wanted to grab my Kindle and scream, "SPEAK ENGLISH, I WANT TO READ YOU!!!". Yes, I understand that the book is written from the POV of a 17 year old. Got it. But she sounds like a damn idiot. Maybe that is what the author is going for. Who the heck knows. But it helps if the reader can comprehend what in the hell is going on and in order to know what is going on, we need to be able to recognize more words than just a handful every couple of pages. <br><br>I absolutely ABHORRED the main character, Lex. She is a self absorbed, neurotic teenager and the way she talks is what is wrong with this generation. I'm not that old and I remember using slang when I was growing up but at least you could still decipher the English language when we talked. She's also crass and immature. You should enjoy reading about people that are different than you, not get annoyed. <br><br>Since I'm talking about characters, the whole beginning thing (I'm not giving away anything that isn't in the blurb or the first chapter) with the boyfriend was just asinine. So this dude is staying in a relationship with Lex but refusing to have sex with her because she's overweight. I call bullshit. No sexually active teenage boy is going to say no to sex when it is being offered up on a silver platter because a chick is ten pounds overweight and then go play hide-the-salami with her coked out, has-been mom. Give me a break. It's just not believable. <br><br>There were also these news articles or statements, I'm not totally sure what they were at this point. Anyway, they were weird because they weren't needed and it drew your attention away from the story as you are trying to figure out why they are included. There were also this dream sequence that literally lasted page after page after page ... it was to the point where you forget that you're reading a dream. I don't know if that is what the author was going for and she was trying to show how off in Lala Land this girl was or what. <br><br>Most authors of YA or New Adult books are in fact, well over the age that they are writing about. There's nothing wrong with that. But there is a problem when it feels like you're insulting that generation with over-usage of nonsensical terms and phrases. Our son is 13 years old and I've been to tons of school functions where hundreds of teenagers are and I've NEVER heard kids use this much slang and improper grammar.<br><br>Ugh. I'll get off my soapbox. Let's just say that it was not the book for me. The truth of the matter is, if I had the option to give it no stars, that's what I would have done this time. I wouldn't recommend it to anyone who enjoys reading New Adult romance novels (or any romance for that matter) and I most certainly will not be picking up another book by this author. Total miss for me. <br><br><i>* I received this novel in exchange for an honest review *</i><br><br>Check out more of my reviews at <a href="http://www.LittleMissBookmark.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Little Miss Bookmark</a>!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12617447237848000096" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_918364981" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/918364981" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2787812-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603811905p2/2787812.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/918364981?book_show_action=true">Apr 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/2787812-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2787812-melanie?shelf=netgallery">netgallery</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer918364981" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7012122801025398343">Stepping away from my usual New Adult books, reading Love, Lex by Avery Aster was a refreshing break and a humorous one at that. I feel I should star this book by saying The Undergrad Years series will NOT be for everyone. If you are offended by certain swear words of a vulgar nature, do not like hearing about drugs, drinking and 'exaggerated' antics of some rich young adults - this book is not for you. However, if you like reading something thats over the top, crazy and has characters that lite</span>
  <span id="freeText7012122801025398343" style="display:none">Stepping away from my usual New Adult books, reading Love, Lex by Avery Aster was a refreshing break and a humorous one at that. I feel I should star this book by saying The Undergrad Years series will NOT be for everyone. If you are offended by certain swear words of a vulgar nature, do not like hearing about drugs, drinking and 'exaggerated' antics of some rich young adults - this book is not for you. However, if you like reading something thats over the top, crazy and has characters that literally jump off the page they are so bright they really are 3D, then I'd give this a go. It is likened to Gossip Girl, being the huge fan I was of GG I disagree or would say GG on some serious Acid.<br /><br />Lex is the child of 2 rock stars, so her upbringing hasn't been perfect and she's a little crazy. But with all that in mind and her crazy antics with her close friends she still managed to keep her 'Lady V' and not lose it yet. Still that was all going to change on her trip to Paris for her 18th birthday with her best friends and boyfriend, that was until she saw said boyfriend screwing her mothers brains out high as a kite and then accidentally setting fire to the apartment. As you can see, from the onset this book was going to be 'out there' and Avery Aster does not disappoint.<br /><br />I really loved the relationships with Lex and her friends, I admit I wasn't that warm to Vive, I found her a little (Ok A LOT) bit of a bitch, but I think there's a lot more going on there and we will find out about that when we get to her story. I did however love Taddy and Blake.. well every girl should have their gay best friend (Trust me, I know that for definite!).<br /><br />Ford was just, well HOT! I loved Lex's day dreams and the incident on the bike towards the end of the book, can I just say 'serious fan moment' I needed some cooling down! It made me chuckle Ford was likened to The Rock 'Dwayne Johnson' as I'm a huge Rock fan (And a closet WWE fan... shhhh) and made the book that much better I had someone to compare Ford too. Also, I loved that Lex was what I call a 'REAL WOMAN' she is super curvy and not perfect, I love reading books in that respect when the leading lady is like the majority of us out there!<br /><br />This book is very tongue in cheek, its not serious and the scenarios are very unlikely to happen. However, it is funny and amusing and kept me happy for the afternoon I read it in. I found it a fairly quick read too and am really looking forward to reading Yours Truly, Taddy shortly.<br /><br />I gave Love, Lex 4 stars because I loved it. It is what it is and as I said at the start of this book it won't appeal to everyone, but for those it does - I'm sure you will love it!<br /><br />Review also featured on my blog - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bewitchedbooks.co.uk/">http://www.bewitchedbooks.co.uk/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7012122801025398343" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_908083465" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/908083465" />
    <a title="Sorcha O&#39;Dowd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11334864-sorcha-o-dowd"><img alt="Sorcha O&#39;Dowd" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442956718p2/11334864.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/908083465?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sorcha O&#39;Dowd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sorcha O&#39;Dowd" href="/user/show/11334864-sorcha-o-dowd">Sorcha O&#39;Dowd</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11334864-sorcha-o-dowd?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11334864-sorcha-o-dowd?shelf=arc-s">arc-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11334864-sorcha-o-dowd?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11334864-sorcha-o-dowd?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11334864-sorcha-o-dowd?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11334864-sorcha-o-dowd?shelf=hea">hea</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11334864-sorcha-o-dowd?shelf=kindle-read">kindle-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11334864-sorcha-o-dowd?shelf=humour">humour</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11334864-sorcha-o-dowd?shelf=crime">crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11334864-sorcha-o-dowd?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer908083465" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3502105618292491096">I can honestly say it’s been a long time since I’ve last laughed so hard whilst reading a book. The last time was with ‘It’s Got to be Perfect’ by Haley Hill (which you should go and read right now). Avery Aster drew me into the story with her clever and witty writing and hilarious characters who you feel like are your own best friends by the end of the book.<br/>If you are looking for an angsty new adult read, then this isn’t for you, but if you just want to sit down with a good, funny book for a fe</span>
  <span id="freeText3502105618292491096" style="display:none">I can honestly say it’s been a long time since I’ve last laughed so hard whilst reading a book. The last time was with ‘It’s Got to be Perfect’ by Haley Hill (which you should go and read right now). Avery Aster drew me into the story with her clever and witty writing and hilarious characters who you feel like are your own best friends by the end of the book.<br />If you are looking for an angsty new adult read, then this isn’t for you, but if you just want to sit down with a good, funny book for a few hours and are in need of a good laugh, then this is definitely a book I’d recommend.<br />Lex was honestly the most bonkers heroine I’ve read of in a while, but even with her craziness I connected with her straight away, and after reading that her boyfriend told her she’d have to lose some weight before he would sleep with her, and her trying her hardest by chewing nicotine gum like it was going out of business was what made me really feel for her, and want the best for her. But the best thing about her was that she didn’t want sympathy or pity, she told the readers how she felt without putting on any masks, and then moved on. <br />The storyline of her being arrested for arson was done in such a brilliant funny way, especially when the story was told to us from Lex’s viewpoint, complete with hilarious acronyms for her best friends (BFF, GFF, GBF, I’ll let you read to find out what the last two stand for) and her complicated relationship with her famous rocker mother (You’ll see what I mean within the first few pages), it really was a light escape to read about. Of course no story is complete without a sexy male, and Officer Gotti fit that role perfectly. <br />This was a crazy story which made me laugh out loud throughout. The main characters were a new definition of crazy, but the fact that they stood by each other in times of crisis helped make the story a little more relatable to the reader and show the seriousness of their situation despite the way they try to cover their feelings with humour and sarcasm.<br />This book was clever, witty, bonkers and just such good fun. If you don’t mind a little over-the-top drama, and some crazy characters, but ones that you really connect with, then this story is the one for you.<br />4 Stars!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3502105618292491096" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText17602907145996761514" style="display:none">Birthdays are meant to be celebrated in style. For Lex and her friends - Taddy, Blake, and Vive - this means spending the summer in Europe. All are excited about their plans….especially Lex. Nothing could put a damper on their plans. <br /><br />Well, almost nothing. Imagine Lex’s surprise to arrive home one afternoon to find her mother in bed with her boyfriend. Birdie’s mission of self gratification has just smacked Lex right in the face. To make matters even worse - Lex decides to ‘purge’ herself of some thing. The result…..Lex is accused of trying to blow up her mother’s penthouse. Of course, her friends are in the slammer with her for their supposed involvement. <br /><br />To make her incarceration a bit more interesting, Lex comes face to face with Officer Ford Gotti. This hunk has Lex desiring more than your basic ‘frisk’. However, Lex’s insecurities promptly make her believe Ford could never be interested in a curvy girl like herself. <br /><br />These Manhattanites will have their friendships and loyalties tested. Officer Gotti is not out of the picture either. How will the girls get out of their predicament? What part will Officer Gotti play in Lex’s endeavors?<br /><br />This novella gives readers a quick glimpse into the wild and crazy life our favorite Manhattanites lead. Each adding a layer to their history and friendship. You can’t read about these friends without a few giggles and a smile on your face!!</span>

  <span id="freeText12688414062604824499" style="display:none">I loved reading Avery Aster's The Manhattanites so reading The Undergrad Years was a no brainer for me. These four delightful friends are so funny and quirky and they draw you into their world with a twist and a shake of sheer cray-cray!!!<br /><br />This story focuses around another near life disaster this time at the hands of Lex. Still trying to put an end to Lady V, she decided that her 18th birthday, in Paris, with her boyfriend , Kelle, is the ideal time to do it. However, her mother, Birdie, has something to say, or rather do, about that! Trying to escape her mother's clutches, Birdie takes matters into her own hands and Birdie nearly falls off her drug induced perch. <br /><br />After all four friends end up on the wrong side of the law, Lex comes face to face with Officer Gotti, a hottie god, and someone who could take down her particulars any time!<br /><br />After being released from the police station, Officer Gotti comes to Lex's assistance, in more ways than one, and soon the two have more than their shared interest of bikes on their minds. <br /><br />This is a quick and easy read and one which, for me, brightened up a dull day. It ends at 85% though, so be warned!<br /><br />Reviewed on behalf of Jezabell Girl &amp; Friends....<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jezabellgirlandfriends.weebly.com">http://jezabellgirlandfriends.weebly.com</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://facebook.com/jezabellgirlandfriends">http://facebook.com/jezabellgirlandfr...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://Twitter.com/Jezabell_girl">http://Twitter.com/Jezabell_girl</a><br /></span>

<div id="review_888861619" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/888861619" />
    <a title="Ava" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18006333-ava"><img alt="Ava" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428584394p2/18006333.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/888861619?book_show_action=true">Mar 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ava" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ava" href="/user/show/18006333-ava">Ava</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer8960731083192196342">When I read Undressed I instantly loved Lex. Some parts I laughed</span>
  <span id="freeText8960731083192196342" style="display:none">When I read Undressed I instantly loved Lex. Avery made her character so real, fun and confident that you knew straight away you could read her story no problem. To read how Lex met her brilliant friends and basically became the way she is later in life was FANTASTIC! <br />Yes in this book she's 18 but she's battling demons we all battle and she's got issues with her mum and boyfriend but it's all dealt with in that sexy, funny, smart way that we've come to love in Avery's books. Some parts I laughed so much I had to explain to others why I was laughing.<br />Oh and then there's Officer God... FREAKING AWESOME! His description alone is pretty amazing.<br />So to keep me tied over I feel I need to go read Undressed again just to get more of the wit, humour, sexiness and perfect friendship that is Lex, Vive, Taddy and Blake.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8960731083192196342" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer916667427" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5238572905332131812">I really liked this. I wish it was longer. Lex has pretty low self-esteem. Both of her parents are rock star so she has been in the eyes of the media since she was a kid. Not as skinny as the other kids she was made fun of for her extra bit of weight. Now the day before her eighteenth birthday, she is trying to lose the weight her scumbag boyfriend told her to lose in order for him to have sex with her. Talk about a low opinion of yourself to even think about agreeing to something like that.<br/><br/>This</span>
  <span id="freeText5238572905332131812" style="display:none">I really liked this. I wish it was longer. Lex has pretty low self-esteem. Both of her parents are rock star so she has been in the eyes of the media since she was a kid. Not as skinny as the other kids she was made fun of for her extra bit of weight. Now the day before her eighteenth birthday, she is trying to lose the weight her scumbag boyfriend told her to lose in order for him to have sex with her. Talk about a low opinion of yourself to even think about agreeing to something like that.<br /><br />This story was interesting from beginning to end. I found that the end was rushed. Regardless, I liked the story. I would love to get to know all the characters in the quartet. You can tell that each character had their own story to tell.<br /><br />Bunnita @ <a href="http://worthreadingit.blogspot.com/2014/04/love-lex-by-avery-aster.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Worth Reading It?</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer921162514" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2748906415068295841">This was 4.5 stars. Love Lex was such a fun, quick read. I liked that I read it after reading Undressed (The Manhattanites #1). In fact, in my opinion you should read Undressed before you read Love Lex. This book has a bit of everything in it. Snark, romance, drama & lots of excitement. <br/><br/>In Love Lex we go back to when she was just turning 18. We see how she deals with a really crappy boyfriend, why her relationship with her mother is so up & down & we also get to see more of Taddy, Vive, & Blake.</span>
  <span id="freeText2748906415068295841" style="display:none">This was 4.5 stars. Love Lex was such a fun, quick read. I liked that I read it after reading Undressed (The Manhattanites #1). In fact, in my opinion you should read Undressed before you read Love Lex. This book has a bit of everything in it. Snark, romance, drama &amp; lots of excitement. <br /><br />In Love Lex we go back to when she was just turning 18. We see how she deals with a really crappy boyfriend, why her relationship with her mother is so up &amp; down &amp; we also get to see more of Taddy, Vive, &amp; Blake. Also, in true Avery Aster fashion this book doesn't lack in the sex department! There's some pretty hot sexy scenes with a tatted up biker cop! It was fun to take a step back in time with Lex and friends.</span>

    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Hi4S2yaveTut02WZmf2rGF3fyrBL0n7ZofpnnF3+h4gkCHsJnfGwUwr40fhuCKHHi4AteIVf8L76hCEtkL11Eg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Qvc4dMuahx86aRjVlh8PErNuEpoDGeLaoEeHArg3xyx40VGmcMROd51CrLRh6gXNZTH1Us2UbL37OcGzdXQ1tg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
